Each pattern includes simple explanations, real-world examples, and practical Java code.</p></div><div class="flex items-center justify-center px-4 max-md:gap-4 max-md:flex-col max-sm:px-0"><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><span class="relative flex shrink-0 overflow-hidden object-cover w-12 h-12 rounded-full max-md:w-10 max-md:h-10"><img class="aspect-square object-cover h-full w-full" alt="Shreya Adak" width="48" height="48" src="https://cs-prod-assets-bucket.s3.ap-south-1.amazonaws.com/Shreya_Adak_min_7895ddc362.png"></span><p class="text-lg font-medium max-md:text-base items-center"><p class="text-lg max-md:text-base text-secondary-blog-text">December 12, 2024</p></div><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-dot mx-2 text-secondary-blog-text"><circle cx="12.1" cy="12.1" r="1"></circle></svg><div class="flex items-center gap-2"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" 3-3h7z"></path></svg><p class="text-lg max-md:text-base text-secondary-blog-text">14 min read</p></div></div></div></div><div class="w-full mx-auto prose prose-lg prose-headings:font-semibold max-w-none prose-headings:leading-snug blog-container dark:prose-invert prose-h2:text-2xl prose-h3:text-xl prose-h4:text-lg"><p>When you're working on any project, writing clean and reusable code becomes important and that's where <strong>design patterns</strong> come in. Also, if you're preparing for an interview, there is a high chance you will be asked to explain some design patterns. For that, having a clear understanding of design patterns is like necessary.</p><p>In this article, I have explained each design pattern in an easy and simple way. I have also included code snippets and <strong>"when to use"</strong> sections for each pattern to help you understand better. So, let's jump into the world of design patterns!</p><h3 id="1-singleton-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>1. Singleton Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#1-singleton-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Singleton Pattern</strong> ensures that a class has <strong>only one instance</strong> throughout the entire application and provides a <strong>global point of access</strong> to that instance. Think of a scenario where you have a single database connection or a configuration manager, you don't want to create multiple objects for these, as they can be heavy and may lead to inconsistencies. That’s where Singleton comes into play.</p><p>In Java, you implement a Singleton by making the constructor <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">private</code>, so no other class can create its object directly. You then create a static method (usually called <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">getInstance()</code>) which will return the same instance every time it's called.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="ldxz5m"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> instance</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">    // private constructor prevents instantiation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Connecting to database..."</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getInstance</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (instance </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">==</span><span style="color:#D19A66"> null</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">            instance </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> instance;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now whenever you need a connection:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="rl79o"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> db1</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getInstance</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> db2</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> DatabaseConnection</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getInstance</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(db1 </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">==</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> db2); </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// true</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Here, <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">db1</code> and <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">db2</code> are both pointing to the <strong>same object</strong>, showing how Singleton avoids multiple object creation. This pattern is useful in logging, configuration classes, and connection pools.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-singleton-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the <strong>Singleton Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-singleton-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When only <strong>one instance</strong> of a class should exist across the application.</li><li>When you need <strong>centralized configuration</strong>, logging, or caching.</li><li>For shared <strong>resources like database connections</strong> or file systems.</li></ul><h3 id="2-factory-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>2. Factory Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#2-factory-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Factory Pattern</strong> helps in creating objects <strong>without exposing the object creation logic</strong> to the client. Instead of using <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">new</code> keyword in different places, you use a factory class to decide which class object should be created, based on input. This becomes extremely useful when you have <strong>multiple subclasses of a parent/interface</strong>, and you want to manage object creation centrally.</p><p>Imagine a graphic design app where users can draw different shapes like circles, squares, or triangles. Rather than creating each shape manually, a factory can handle it.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="f08ko8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Shape</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> draw</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Circle</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Shape</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> draw</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Drawing Circle"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Square</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Shape</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> draw</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Drawing Square"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> ShapeFactory</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Shape</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getShape</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> type</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#98C379">"circle"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">equalsIgnoreCase</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(type)) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Circle</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        } </span><span style="color:#C678DD">else</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#98C379">"square"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">equalsIgnoreCase</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(type)) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Square</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#D19A66"> null</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Client usage becomes easy and clean:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="4upqn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Shape</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> shape1</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> ShapeFactory</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getShape</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"circle"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        shape1</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">draw</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(); </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Drawing Circle</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Shape</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> shape2</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> ShapeFactory</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getShape</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"square"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        shape2</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">draw</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(); </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Drawing Square</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>This pattern is great when the logic to create an object is complex or involves decision-making. It also keeps your code <strong>open for extension but closed for modification</strong>, which is one of the SOLID principles.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-factory-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the <strong>Factory Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-factory-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When object creation logic is <strong>complex</strong> or involves <strong>decision-making</strong>.</li><li>When you want to create objects <strong>without exposing the actual class</strong>.</li><li>When you need <strong>loose coupling</strong> between client code and actual implementations.</li></ul><h3 id="3-builder-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>3. Builder Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#3-builder-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Builder Pattern</strong> is perfect when you need to construct <strong>complex objects step-by-step</strong>, especially if some fields are optional. It helps you avoid the problem of <strong>constructor overloading</strong>, where you end up writing multiple constructors with different parameter combinations.</p><p>Let’s say you’re building a <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">User</code> object where some properties like <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">name</code> and <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">email</code> are required, but others like <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">age</code>, <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">phone</code>, or <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">address</code> are optional. The builder pattern makes this process more readable and less error-prone.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="w7gpbv"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> User</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> name</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> email</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> int</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> age</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> User</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">UserBuilder</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> builder</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">name</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> builder</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">name</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">email</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> builder</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">email</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">age</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> builder</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">age</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> UserBuilder</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> name</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> email</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        private</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> int</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> age</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> UserBuilder</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> setName</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> name</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">name</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> name;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> UserBuilder</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> setEmail</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> email</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">email</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> email;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> UserBuilder</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> setAge</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">int</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> age</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">age</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> age;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> User</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> build</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> User</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> toString</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> name </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> " | "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> email </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> " | "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> age;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>You can now build an object like this:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="ths2u"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        User</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> user</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> User.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">UserBuilder</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">                .</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">setName</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Munaf"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">                .</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">setEmail</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"munaf@example.com"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">                .</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">setAge</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#D19A66">18</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">                .</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">build</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(user);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>The Builder pattern makes your code <strong>cleaner, more readable, and flexible</strong>, especially for creating DTOs or response models in large applications.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-builder-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Builder <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-builder-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When you need to <strong>build complex objects</strong> with many optional parameters.</li><li>When object creation requires a <strong>step-by-step process</strong>.</li><li>To avoid constructor overload with many parameters.</li></ul><h3 id="4-prototype-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>4. Prototype Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#4-prototype-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Prototype Pattern</strong> is used when you want to <strong>create a copy of an existing object</strong> instead of building a new one from scratch. It’s very useful when object creation is <strong>expensive or time-consuming</strong>, like when loading from a database or performing deep configuration.</p><p>In Java, this pattern uses the <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">clone()</code> method (from <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">Cloneable</code> interface) to make a duplicate of an object.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="8iyt65"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Vehicle</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Cloneable</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> type</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Vehicle</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> type</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">type</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> type;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Vehicle</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> clone</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        try</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (Vehicle) </span><span style="color:#E5C07B">super</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">clone</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        } </span><span style="color:#C678DD">catch</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">CloneNotSupportedException</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> e</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            return</span><span style="color:#D19A66"> null</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> setType</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> type</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">type</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> type;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> toString</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#98C379"> "Vehicle: "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> type;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Here’s how it works:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="zilqlb"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Vehicle</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> car</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Vehicle</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Car"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Vehicle</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> carCopy</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> car</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">clone</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        carCopy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">setType</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Bike"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(car);      </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Vehicle: Car</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(carCopy);  </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Vehicle: Bike</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Notice how cloning saves time by copying an existing object. The Prototype pattern is used in real-world apps where object configuration is heavy, and you want to quickly make a copy and just tweak a few things.</p><p>Perfect! Let’s continue our blog with the remaining <strong>4 Java design patterns</strong> in the same beginner-friendly, paragraph style — keeping it simple, practical, and code-backed.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-prototype-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Prototype <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-prototype-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When object creation is <strong>expensive</strong> or <strong>time-consuming</strong>.</li><li>When you need to create <strong>many copies of similar objects</strong>.</li><li>To <strong>clone existing objects</strong> instead of building new ones from scratch.</li></ul><h3 id="5-adapter-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>5. Adapter Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#5-adapter-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Adapter Pattern</strong> is used when you want to <strong>make two incompatible interfaces work together</strong>. It acts like a bridge or a connector between two classes that otherwise cannot communicate. Imagine you bought a charger from the US, but you’re in India — an adapter allows it to fit the socket here. This design pattern does the same with classes.</p><p>In Java, this is commonly used when integrating third-party APIs or legacy code with your new system.</p><p>Let’s say you have an <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">AdvancedMediaPlayer</code> which supports only <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">.vlc</code> and <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">.mp4</code> files, but your application uses a generic <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">MediaPlayer</code> interface.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="lzg9jl"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> MediaPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> play</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> audioType</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">, </span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> fileName</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> VlcPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> playVlc</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> fileName</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Playing VLC file: "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> fileName);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> VlcAdapter</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> MediaPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> VlcPlayer</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> vlcPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> VlcAdapter</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        vlcPlayer </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> VlcPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> play</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> audioType</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">, </span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> fileName</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#98C379">"vlc"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">equalsIgnoreCase</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(audioType)) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            vlcPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">playVlc</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(fileName);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now we plug this adapter into our application:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="gm10zi"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> AudioPlayer</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> MediaPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> play</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> audioType</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">, </span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> fileName</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#98C379">"mp3"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">equalsIgnoreCase</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(audioType)) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Playing MP3 file: "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> fileName);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        } </span><span style="color:#C678DD">else</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#98C379">"vlc"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">equalsIgnoreCase</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(audioType)) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            MediaPlayer</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> adapter</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> VlcAdapter</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            adapter</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">play</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(audioType, fileName);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        } </span><span style="color:#C678DD">else</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Format not supported"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Usage:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="l8o62k"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        AudioPlayer</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> player</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> AudioPlayer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        player</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">play</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"mp3"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">, </span><span style="color:#98C379">"song.mp3"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        player</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">play</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"vlc"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">, </span><span style="color:#98C379">"video.vlc"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>This pattern is perfect when you're dealing with legacy code or third-party tools that don’t directly match your interface needs.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-adapter-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Adapter <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-adapter-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When two classes <strong>don’t match interfaces</strong> but need to work together.</li><li>When integrating with <strong>legacy code</strong> or <strong>third-party libraries</strong>.</li><li>To make existing classes <strong>compatible with new code</strong>.</li></ul><h3 id="6-observer-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>6. Observer Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#6-observer-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Observer Pattern</strong> defines a one-to-many relationship between objects. When <strong>one object changes</strong>, all its dependent objects (observers) are <strong>automatically notified and updated</strong>. You’ve definitely seen this in real life — for example, subscribing to a YouTube channel. Once the channel posts a video, all subscribers get notified.</p><p>This is very common in event-driven systems, UI frameworks, and messaging systems.</p><p>Let’s see how this works in Java:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="87co9l"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">import</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> java.util.*</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Observer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> update</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> message</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Subscriber</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Observer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> name</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Subscriber</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> name</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">name</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> name;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> update</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> message</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(name </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> " received: "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> message);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now we need a <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">Subject</code> that notifies subscribers:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="h5ikq8"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Channel</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> List</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">&lt;</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Observer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">&gt;</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> subscribers </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> ArrayList</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">&lt;&gt;</span><span style="color:#E06C75">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> subscribe</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Observer</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> observer</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        subscribers</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">add</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(observer);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> notifyAllSubscribers</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> message</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        for</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Observer</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> obs</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> :</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> subscribers) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            obs</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">update</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(message);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Usage:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="35719p"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Channel</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> codingShuttle</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Channel</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Subscriber</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> s1</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Subscriber</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Munaf"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Subscriber</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> s2</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Subscriber</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Ravi"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        codingShuttle</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">subscribe</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(s1);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        codingShuttle</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">subscribe</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(s2);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        codingShuttle</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">notifyAllSubscribers</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"New Spring Boot video is live!"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
