<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>This pattern keeps your code <strong>loosely coupled</strong>, and is useful in applications where data change needs to be broadcasted — like stock prices, chat apps, and notification systems.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-observer-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Observer <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-observer-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When <strong>multiple objects</strong> need to be notified when <strong>one object changes</strong>.</li><li>In <strong>event-driven systems</strong> like GUIs, chat apps, or notification systems.</li><li>When implementing <strong>publish-subscribe</strong> behavior.</li></ul><h3 id="7-strategy-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>7. Strategy Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#7-strategy-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Strategy Pattern</strong> is all about <strong>choosing a behavior at runtime</strong>. Instead of writing complex <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">if-else</code> or <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">switch</code> statements, you define multiple strategies (algorithms), and select one dynamically.</p><p>Let’s say you’re building a payment system that supports different methods: Credit Card, UPI, or PayPal. Using strategy pattern, you can switch between these strategies easily without changing core logic.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="nftnq7"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> PaymentStrategy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> pay</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">double</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> amount</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> CreditCardPayment</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> PaymentStrategy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> pay</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">double</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> amount</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Paid ₹"</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> amount </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> " using Credit Card"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> UPIPayment</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> PaymentStrategy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> pay</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">double</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> amount</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Paid ₹"</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> amount </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> " using UPI"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now we plug this into a <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">PaymentService</code> class:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="xml806"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> PaymentService</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> PaymentStrategy</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> strategy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> PaymentService</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">PaymentStrategy</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> strategy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">strategy</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> strategy;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> makePayment</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">double</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> amount</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        strategy</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">pay</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(amount);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Usage:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="v91kl4"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        PaymentService</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> service1</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> PaymentService</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> CreditCardPayment</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        service1</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">makePayment</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#D19A66">2500</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        PaymentService</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> service2</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> PaymentService</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#C678DD">new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> UPIPayment</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        service2</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">makePayment</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#D19A66">1200</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>This pattern helps in <strong>separating different behaviors</strong>, making the code <strong>easier to extend and test</strong>. You can add a new payment method without touching any existing code.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-strategy-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Strategy <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-strategy-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When you need to <strong>choose behavior/algorithm at runtime</strong>.</li><li>To eliminate long <strong>if-else</strong> or <strong>switch</strong> statements.</li><li>When you want to make a class <strong>open to extension but closed to modification</strong>.</li></ul><h3 id="8-decorator-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>8. Decorator Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#8-decorator-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Decorator Pattern</strong> is used to <strong>dynamically add new functionality</strong> to an object without modifying its original code. It’s like adding toppings on a pizza — the base remains the same, but you can add cheese, mushrooms, or paneer to customize it.</p><p>Let’s build a simple coffee ordering system where you can add milk, sugar, etc., on top of base coffee.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="cdo10q"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">    String</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getDescription</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    double</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> SimpleCoffee</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getDescription</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#98C379"> "Simple Coffee"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> double</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#D19A66"> 50</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now let’s add decorators:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="g6ql0k"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" <span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getDescription</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">() </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> ", Milk"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> double</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">() </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#D19A66"> 10</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> SugarDecorator</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">coffee</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> coffee;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> String</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getDescription</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getDescription</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">() </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#98C379"> ", Sugar"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> double</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        return</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">() </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">+</span><span style="color:#D19A66"> 5</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Usage:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="4m958"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Coffee</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> coffee</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> SimpleCoffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        coffee </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> MilkDecorator</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(coffee);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        coffee </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> SugarDecorator</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(coffee);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Order: "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getDescription</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Cost: ₹"</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> coffee</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getCost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Output:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="2689bl"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span>Order: Simple Coffee, Milk, Sugar</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>Cost: ₹65.0</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>The Decorator pattern is very powerful when you want to add features <strong>without altering the existing code</strong>, and is commonly used in logging, security, and user interface designs.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-decorator-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Decorator <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-decorator-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When you want to <strong>add responsibilities/features dynamically</strong> to an object.</li><li>To <strong>extend functionality</strong> without modifying the original class.</li><li>For <strong>flexible and reusable wrappers</strong> (e.g., UI components, logging).</li></ul><h3 id="9-proxy-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>9. Proxy Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#9-proxy-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Proxy Pattern</strong> provides a <strong>placeholder or substitute</strong> for another object to control access to it. Think of it like a receptionist at a company. You don’t directly talk to the boss — the receptionist acts as a <strong>middle layer</strong> to either pass the message or deny access.</p><p>This pattern is especially useful in cases like <strong>lazy initialization</strong>, <strong>access control</strong>, <strong>caching</strong>, or <strong>logging</strong>. You wrap the original object with another class (the proxy) and intercept calls to it.</p><p>Let’s take an example of an <code class="bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 rounded-sm p-[2px] break-all">Internet</code> interface where access to certain websites is restricted.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="uhuvoe"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Internet</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> connectTo</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> serverHost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> throws</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Exception</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now the actual internet class:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="7ax6i"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> RealInternet</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Internet</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> connectTo</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> serverHost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Connecting to "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> serverHost);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Let’s create a proxy that adds restrictions:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="iuaf7r"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">import</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> java.util.*</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> ProxyInternet</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Internet</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Internet</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> internet </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> RealInternet</span><span style="color:#E06C75">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> List</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">&lt;</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">&gt;</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> bannedSites</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    static</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E06C75">        bannedSites </span><span style="color:#56B6C2">=</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> ArrayList</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">&lt;&gt;</span><span style="color:#E06C75">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        bannedSites</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">add</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"facebook.com"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        bannedSites</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">add</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"instagram.com"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E06C75">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> connectTo</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> serverHost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> throws</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Exception</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        if</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">bannedSites</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">contains</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">serverHost</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">toLowerCase</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">())) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">            throw</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Exception</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Access Denied to "</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> +</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> serverHost);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        internet</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">connectTo</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(serverHost);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Usage:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="vo9o2l"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Internet</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> net</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> ProxyInternet</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">        try</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            net</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">connectTo</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"google.com"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);        </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Allowed</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            net</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">connectTo</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"facebook.com"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);      </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Blocked</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        } </span><span style="color:#C678DD">catch</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> (</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Exception</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> e</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">            System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">e</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">getMessage</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>This pattern is commonly used in frameworks like Spring AOP, where proxy classes wrap services to add logging, security, or transactional behavior.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-proxy-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Proxy <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-proxy-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When you want to <strong>control access</strong> to another object.</li><li>For <strong>lazy loading</strong>, <strong>caching</strong>, <strong>logging</strong>, or <strong>security checks</strong>.</li><li>When adding a <strong>middle layer</strong> between client and real object.</li></ul><h3 id="10-command-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6"><strong>10. Command Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#10-command-pattern">#</a></h3><p>The <strong>Command Pattern</strong> is used to <strong>encapsulate a request as an object</strong>, allowing us to parameterize clients with different requests, queue them, or log them. Think of it like placing an order at a restaurant — the waiter (command object) takes the order and passes it to the kitchen (receiver) without the customer needing to know how it’s cooked.</p><p>This is very useful in <strong>UI buttons, undo/redo operations, task scheduling</strong>, and even <strong>remote controls</strong>.</p><p>Let’s see an example of a remote control turning devices ON/OFF.</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="0yzarl"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">interface</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Command</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> execute</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> turnOn</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Light turned ON"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> turnOff</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        System</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">out</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">println</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#98C379">"Light turned OFF"</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Now we create command objects:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="19s3pd"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> LightOnCommand</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Command</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Light</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> LightOnCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Light</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">light</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> light;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> execute</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">turnOn</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> LightOffCommand</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> implements</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Command</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Light</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> LightOffCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Light</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">light</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> light;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> execute</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">turnOff</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>And finally, a simple remote control to trigger these:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="da8ac"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> RemoteControl</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    private</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Command</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> command</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> setCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">Command</span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic"> command</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        this</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">command</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> command;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> pressButton</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">()</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        command</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">execute</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>Usage:</p><pre class="border text-[#e5e7eb] border-blog-border not-prose text-base rounded-lg my-4 p-0 relative !bg-[#0F172A] dark:!bg-[#07090F] grid"><div class="absolute z-[2] top-2.5 right-3"><button aria-checked="false" class="relative group flex items-center justify-center border border-gray-600 rounded-lg w-9 h-9" fdprocessedid="9luj4"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy text-gray-600 transition-all duration-300 group-hover:text-blue-500 group-aria-checked:scale-0"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check absolute transition-transform duration-300 scale-0 -translate-y-1/2 top-2/4 text-success group-aria-checked:scale-100"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg></button></div><div dir="ltr" class="relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-full p-4" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="h-full w-full rounded-[inherit]" style="overflow: scroll;"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><div class="!bg-inherit pb-0 "><div><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> class</span><span style="color:#E5C07B"> Main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#C678DD">    public</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> static</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> void</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> main</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(</span><span style="color:#E5C07B">String</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">[] </span><span style="color:#E06C75;font-style:italic">args</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">)</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Light</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> livingRoomLight</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> Light</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Command</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> on</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> LightOnCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(livingRoomLight);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        Command</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> off</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> LightOffCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(livingRoomLight);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        RemoteControl</span><span style="color:#E06C75"> remote</span><span style="color:#56B6C2"> =</span><span style="color:#C678DD"> new</span><span style="color:#61AFEF"> RemoteControl</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        remote</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">setCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(on);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        remote</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">pressButton</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();  </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Light turned ON</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        remote</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">setCommand</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">(off);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E5C07B">        remote</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">.</span><span style="color:#61AFEF">pressButton</span><span style="color:#ABB2BF">();  </span><span style="color:#7F848E;font-style:italic">// Light turned OFF</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#ABB2BF">}</span></span></code></div></div></div></div></div></pre><p>This pattern is helpful when you need to <strong>separate the object that invokes a command from the one that knows how to perform it</strong>, making your code more flexible and modular.</p><h3 id="when-to-use-the-command-pattern" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">When to use the Command <strong>Pattern</strong><a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#when-to-use-the-command-pattern">#</a></h3><ul><li>When you need to <strong>encapsulate actions/operations as objects</strong>.</li><li>For <strong>undo/redo</strong>, <strong>task queues</strong>, or <strong>remote execution</strong>.</li><li>When you want to <strong>decouple the sender and receiver</strong> of a request.</li></ul><h3 id="conclusion" class="relative group scroll-mt-6">Conclusion<a aria-label="jump-to-section-links" class="pl-2 font-bold no-underline opacity-0 hover:underline text-primary group-hover:opacity-100" href="#conclusion">#</a></h3><p>Finally, we have covered 10 of the most popular design patterns that are widely used in real-world projects and often asked in interviews. I hope you now have a clear picture in your mind of how each design pattern works. I also suggest practicing each design pattern on your own to understand it better and apply it effectively in your code.</p><div class="pl-3 my-6 space-y-1 border-l-4 rounded not-prose"><h4 class="text-lg font-semibold text-primary-blog-text">Want to Master Spring Boot and Land Your Dream Job?</h4><p class="text-base">Struggling with coding interviews?
