class="hljs-type">DepartmentHead</span> <span class="hljs-variable">departmentHead</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">DepartmentHead</span>();<br><br>        teamLead.setNextApprover(manager);<br>        manager.setNextApprover(departmentHead);<br><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Create and process leave requests</span><br>        <span class="hljs-type">LeaveRequest</span> <span class="hljs-variable">request1</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">LeaveRequest</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"John"</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>);<br>        <span class="hljs-type">LeaveRequest</span> <span class="hljs-variable">request2</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">LeaveRequest</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Alice"</span>, <span class="hljs-number">7</span>);<br>        <span class="hljs-type">LeaveRequest</span> <span class="hljs-variable">request3</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">LeaveRequest</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Bob"</span>, <span class="hljs-number">12</span>);<br><br>        teamLead.approveLeave(request1);<br>        teamLead.approveLeave(request2);<br>        teamLead.approveLeave(request3);<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><p id="141c" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">By implementing the Chain of Responsibility pattern, we achieved a flexible and decoupled solution where multiple handlers can process a request in a sequential manner. This pattern promotes scalability and maintainability by allowing new handlers to be added or existing ones to be modified without affecting the client code. Understanding and applying the Chain of Responsibility pattern can greatly enhance the design and architecture of software systems, especially those with complex request handling workflows.</p><h2 id="d5d1" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">4. Command Pattern</h2><p id="7b83" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">The Command pattern <strong class="mr gs">encapsulates a request as an object, thereby allowing parameterization of clients with queues, requests, and operations.</strong> It decouples the sender of a request from its receiver, enabling the requester to send a command without knowing anything about the operation that will be performed.</p><div class="qe v"><div class="e"><a class="z ab ac fg af ag ah ai aj ak al am an ao ap v" rel="noopener follow" href="/download-app?source=promotion_paragraph---post_body_banner_better_screentime--7551731091fd---------------------------------------" data-discover="true"><picture><source media="(max-width: 551.98px)" srcset="https://miro.medium.com/v2/da:true/resize:fit:0/15ae17c70baeeb130e8acca0a0db34f7dbdc48ad3b7ce7da26b5e3e63f94be42"><source media="(min-width: 552px) and (max-width: 727.98px)" srcset="https://miro.medium.com/v2/da:true/resize:fit:0/15ae17c70baeeb130e8acca0a0db34f7dbdc48ad3b7ce7da26b5e3e63f94be42"><source media="(min-width: 728px) and (max-width: 903.98px)" srcset="https://miro.medium.com/v2/da:true/resize:fit:0/b45a35cf900895c2a6f4c9db90ee725dd016aef7b67da1455d7849701f1562f1"><source media="(min-width: 904px) and (max-width: 1079.98px)" srcset="https://miro.medium.com/v2/da:true/resize:fit:0/b45a35cf900895c2a6f4c9db90ee725dd016aef7b67da1455d7849701f1562f1"><source media="(min-width: 1080px)" srcset="https://miro.medium.com/v2/da:true/resize:fit:0/b45a35cf900895c2a6f4c9db90ee725dd016aef7b67da1455d7849701f1562f1"><img alt="Download the Medium App" class="bd" loading="lazy"></picture></a></div></div><p id="08ab" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mu mv mw my mz na nc nd ne ng nh ni nk nl qe nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Let’s consider a real-time example of a remote control for electronic devices to understand the Command pattern in action. In this scenario:</p><ul class=""><li id="804f" class="mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Command: </strong>Each button on the remote control represents a command (e.g., turn on, turn off, increase volume, decrease volume).</li><li id="bf05" class="mp mq gr mr b ms pk mu mv mw pl my mz na pm nc nd ne pn ng nh ni po nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Receiver:</strong> The electronic devices (e.g., TV, stereo system) are the receivers of the commands. They perform the requested operations.</li></ul><h2 id="52d2" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Implementation Steps</h2><p id="1b9d" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Now, let’s walk through the steps to implement the Command pattern for the remote control system in Java:</p><h3 id="37fe" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 1: Define the Command Interface</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="e1e8" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title">Command</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">execute</span>()</span>;<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="c2a6" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 2: Implement Concrete Commands</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="f09b" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TurnOnCommand</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Command</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> ElectronicDevice device;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">TurnOnCommand</span><span class="hljs-params">(ElectronicDevice device)</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-built_in">this</span>.device = device;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">execute</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {<br>        device.turnOn();<br>    }<br>}<br><br><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TurnOffCommand</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Command</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> ElectronicDevice device;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">TurnOffCommand</span><span class="hljs-params">(ElectronicDevice device)</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-built_in">this</span>.device = device;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">execute</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {<br>        device.turnOff();<br>    }<br>}<br><br><span class="hljs-comment">// Additional commands (e.g., IncreaseVolumeCommand, DecreaseVolumeCommand) can be implemented similarly.</span></span></pre><h3 id="598a" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 3: Define the Receiver</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="a282" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">ElectronicDevice</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> String name;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title">ElectronicDevice</span>(<span class="hljs-params">String name</span>)</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.name = name;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">turnOn</span>()</span> {<br>        System.<span class="hljs-keyword">out</span>.println(name + <span class="hljs-string">" is turned on."</span>);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">turnOff</span>()</span> {<br>        System.<span class="hljs-keyword">out</span>.println(name + <span class="hljs-string">" is turned off."</span>);<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="2657" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 4: Create the Invoker (Remote Control)</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="1316" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">RemoteControl</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Command</span> command;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">setCommand</span>(<span class="hljs-params">Command command</span>) {<br>        <span class="hljs-variable.language">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">command</span> = command;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">pressButton</span>() {<br>        command.<span class="hljs-title.function">execute</span>();<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="a660" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 5: Test the Implementation</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="775b" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Main</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">main</span><span class="hljs-params">(String[] args)</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-type">ElectronicDevice</span> <span class="hljs-variable">tv</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">ElectronicDevice</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"TV"</span>);<br>        <span class="hljs-type">TurnOnCommand</span> <span class="hljs-variable">turnOnCommand</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TurnOnCommand</span>(tv);<br>        <span class="hljs-type">TurnOffCommand</span> <span class="hljs-variable">turnOffCommand</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TurnOffCommand</span>(tv);<br><br>        <span class="hljs-type">RemoteControl</span> <span class="hljs-variable">remoteControl</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">RemoteControl</span>();<br><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Set and press the turn on button</span><br>        remoteControl.setCommand(turnOnCommand);<br>        remoteControl.pressButton();<br><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Set and press the turn off button</span><br>        remoteControl.setCommand(turnOffCommand);<br>        remoteControl.pressButton();<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><p id="e0ab" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">By implementing the Command pattern, we achieved a flexible and decoupled solution where the requester (remote control) sends a command to the receiver (electronic device) without knowing the specific operation that will be performed. This pattern promotes extensibility and scalability by allowing new commands to be added easily without modifying existing client code. Understanding and applying the Command pattern can greatly enhance the design and architecture of software systems, especially those with complex command execution workflows.</p><h2 id="6169" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">5. Iterator Pattern</h2><p id="b8d3" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">The Iterator pattern <strong class="mr gs">provides a way to access the elements of a collection sequentially without exposing its underlying representation.</strong> It allows for traversal of elements in a collection without exposing the underlying data structure, thus promoting encapsulation and decoupling between the collection and the client code.</p><p id="0265" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Let’s consider a real-time example of a music playlist management system to understand the Iterator pattern in action. In this scenario:</p><ul class=""><li id="7f50" class="mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Collection:</strong> The music playlist represents a collection of songs.</li><li id="2269" class="mp mq gr mr b ms pk mu mv mw pl my mz na pm nc nd ne pn ng nh ni po nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Iterator:</strong> The iterator provides a way to traverse through the songs in the playlist without exposing the playlist’s internal structure.</li></ul><h2 id="05cc" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Implementation Steps</h2><p id="1d94" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Now, let’s walk through the steps to implement the Iterator pattern for the music playlist management system in Java:</p><h3 id="1841" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 1: Define the Iterator Interface</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="0299" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title">Iterator</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-function">boolean <span class="hljs-title">hasNext</span>()</span>;<br>    <span class="hljs-function">Object <span class="hljs-title">next</span>()</span>;<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="cede" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 2: Implement Concrete Iterator</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="882b" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">SongIterator</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Iterator</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span>[] songs;<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> int position = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">SongIterator</span>(<span class="hljs-title.class">String</span>[] songs) {<br>        <span class="hljs-variable.language">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">songs</span> = songs;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">boolean</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">hasNext</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> position &lt; songs.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> &amp;&amp; songs[position] != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Object</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">next</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span> song = songs[position];<br>        position++;<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> song;<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="5208" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 3: Define the Aggregate Interface</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="39d0" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title">Playlist</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-function">Iterator <span class="hljs-title">createIterator</span>()</span>;<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="727c" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 4: Implement Concrete Aggregate</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="c311" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">MusicPlaylist</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Playlist</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span>[] songs;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">MusicPlaylist</span>(<span class="hljs-title.class">String</span>[] songs) {<br>        <span class="hljs-variable.language">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">songs</span> = songs;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Iterator</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">createIterator</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">SongIterator</span>(songs);<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="d7c7" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 5: Test the Implementation</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="629f" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Main</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">main</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">String</span>[] args</span>) {<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span>[] songs = {<span class="hljs-string">"Song 1"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Song 2"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Song 3"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Song 4"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Song 5"</span>};<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">Playlist</span> playlist = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">MusicPlaylist</span>(songs);<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">Iterator</span> iterator = playlist.<span class="hljs-title.function">createIterator</span>();<br><br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">System</span>.<span class="hljs-property">out</span>.<span class="hljs-title.function">println</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Playlist Songs:"</span>);<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (iterator.<span class="hljs-title.function">hasNext</span>()) {<br>            <span class="hljs-title.class">System</span>.<span class="hljs-property">out</span>.<span class="hljs-title.function">println</span>(iterator.<span class="hljs-title.function">next</span>());<br>        }<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><p id="e668" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">By implementing the Iterator pattern, we achieved a flexible and decoupled solution where the client code can traverse through the collection of songs without knowing the internal representation of the playlist. This pattern promotes encapsulation and abstraction, allowing for seamless iteration over different types of collections. Understanding and applying the Iterator pattern can greatly enhance the design and usability of software systems dealing with collections and aggregates.</p><h2 id="07e0" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">6. Memento Pattern</h2><p id="79a9" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">The Memento pattern <strong class="mr gs">allows the capture and externalization of an object’s internal state so that it can be restored later without violating encapsulation. </strong>It is useful when implementing features like undo mechanisms or restoring objects to a previous state.</p><p id="20ca" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Let’s consider a real-time example of a text editor with an undo mechanism to understand the Memento pattern in action. In this scenario:</p><ul class=""><li id="b470" class="mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Originator: </strong>The text editor represents the originator. It has an internal state (text content) that can be modified.</li><li id="e7d8" class="mp mq gr mr b ms pk mu mv mw pl my mz na pm nc nd ne pn ng nh ni po nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Memento:</strong> The memento object captures the state of the text editor at a specific point in time.</li><li id="0726" class="mp mq gr mr b ms pk mu mv mw pl my mz na pm nc nd ne pn ng nh ni po nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Caretaker:</strong> The caretaker manages the mementos and is responsible for saving and restoring the state of the text editor.</li></ul><h2 id="b578" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Implementation Steps</h2><p id="8f0b" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Now, let’s walk through the steps to implement the Memento pattern for the text editor undo mechanism in Java:</p><h3 id="3a51" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 1: Define the Memento</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="6a4f" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditorMemento</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span> text;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditorMemento</span>(<span class="hljs-title.class">String</span> text) {<br>        <span class="hljs-variable.language">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">text</span> = text;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">getText</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> text;<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="2613" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 2: Define the Originator</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="f2b3" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditor</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">String</span> text;<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">setText</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">String</span> text</span>) {<br>        <span class="hljs-variable.language">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">text</span> = text;<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditorMemento</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">save</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditorMemento</span>(text);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">restore</span>(<span class="hljs-params">TextEditorMemento memento</span>) {<br>        <span class="hljs-variable.language">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">text</span> = memento.<span class="hljs-title.function">getText</span>();<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">printText</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">System</span>.<span class="hljs-property">out</span>.<span class="hljs-title.function">println</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Current Text: "</span> + text);<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="9ac6" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 3: Define the Caretaker</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="4279" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.util.Stack;<br><br><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditorHistory</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> Stack&lt;TextEditorMemento&gt; history = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Stack</span>&lt;&gt;();<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">save</span><span class="hljs-params">(TextEditorMemento memento)</span> {<br>        history.push(memento);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> TextEditorMemento <span class="hljs-title.function">undo</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!history.isEmpty()) {<br>            <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> history.pop();<br>        }<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="a859" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 4: Test the Implementation</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="b7eb" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Main</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">main</span><span class="hljs-params">(String[] args)</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-type">TextEditor</span> <span class="hljs-variable">textEditor</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditor</span>();<br>        <span class="hljs-type">TextEditorHistory</span> <span class="hljs-variable">history</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">TextEditorHistory</span>();<br><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Set initial text</span><br>        textEditor.setText(<span class="hljs-string">"Hello World!"</span>);<br>        textEditor.printText();<br><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Save state and modify text</span><br>        history.save(textEditor.save());<br>        textEditor.setText(<span class="hljs-string">"Updated Text"</span>);<br>        textEditor.printText();<br><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Undo and restore previous state</span><br>        <span class="hljs-type">TextEditorMemento</span> <span class="hljs-variable">memento</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> history.undo();<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (memento != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {<br>            textEditor.restore(memento);<br>        }<br>        textEditor.printText();<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><p id="3a28" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">By implementing the Memento pattern, we achieved a solution that allows capturing and restoring the state of the text editor without exposing its internal details. This pattern promotes encapsulation and provides a convenient way to implement features like undo functionalities. Understanding and applying the Memento pattern can greatly enhance the design and usability of software systems requiring state management and history tracking.</p><h2 id="a95d" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">7. Template Method</h2><p id="30fa" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">The Template Method pattern <strong class="mr gs">defines the skeleton of an algorithm in the superclass but lets subclasses override specific steps of the algorithm without changing its structure.</strong> It enables code reuse and promotes consistent behavior across subclasses while allowing for customization of certain steps.</p><p id="2d35" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Let’s consider a real-time example of a beverage brewing process to understand the Template Method pattern in action. In this scenario:</p><ul class=""><li id="a10b" class="mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Abstract Class: </strong>The beverage class represents an abstract class defining the template method for brewing a beverage.</li><li id="7314" class="mp mq gr mr b ms pk mu mv mw pl my mz na pm nc nd ne pn ng nh ni po nk nl nm pp pi pj bg" data-selectable-paragraph=""><strong class="mr gs">Concrete Classes:</strong> Subclasses like Coffee and Tea extend the abstract class and provide implementations for specific steps of the brewing process.</li></ul><h2 id="c1d9" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Implementation Steps</h2><p id="02fa" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Now, let’s walk through the steps to implement the Template Method pattern for the beverage brewing process in Java:</p><h3 id="92e1" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 1: Define the Abstract Class</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="4453" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">Beverage</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-comment">// Template method defining the brewing process</span><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> final <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">brew</span>()</span> {<br>        boilWater();<br>        addIngredients();<br>        pourInCup();<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (customerWantsCondiments()) {<br>            addCondiments();<br>        }<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-comment">// Abstract methods to be implemented by subclasses</span><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">addIngredients</span>()</span>;<br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">abstract</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span water"</span>);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">pourInCup</span>()</span> {<br>        System.<span class="hljs-keyword">out</span>.println(<span class="hljs-string">"Pouring into cup"</span>);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-comment">// Hook method (optional override)</span><br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> boolean <span class="hljs-title">customerWantsCondiments</span>()</span> {<br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>;<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="bfa2" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 2: Implement Concrete Classes</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="ecd4" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Coffee</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">addCondiments</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">System</span>.<span class="hljs-property">out</span>.<span class="hljs-title.function">println</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Adding sugar and milk"</span>);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">boolean</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">customerWantsCondiments</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Override hook method to ask user for condiments preference</span><br>        <span class="hljs-comment">// Return true for coffee by default</span><br>        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>;<br>    }<br>}<br><br><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title.class">Tea</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title.class.inherited">Beverage</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">addIngredients</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">System</span>.<span class="hljs-property">out</span>.<span class="hljs-title.function">println</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Adding tea leaves"</span>);<br>    }<br><br>    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span><br>    <span class="hljs-keyword">protected</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">void</span> <span class="hljs-title.function">addCondiments</span>() {<br>        <span class="hljs-title.class">System</span>.<span class="hljs-property">out</span>.<span class="hljs-title.function">println</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Adding lemon"</span>);<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><h3 id="c49c" class="oq no gr bb np or os ot nt ou ov ow nx na ox oy oz ne pa pb pc ni pd pe pf pg bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Step 3: Test the Implementation</h3><pre class="pq pr ps pt pu pv pw px bl py ax bg"><span id="8ce3" class="pz no gr pw b bc qa qb e qc qd" data-selectable-paragraph=""><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">Main</span> {<br>    <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title">main</span>(<span class="hljs-params">String[] args</span>)</span> {<br>        Beverage coffee = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> Coffee();<br>        Beverage tea = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> Tea();<br><br>        System.<span class="hljs-keyword">out</span>.println(<span class="hljs-string">"Making Coffee:"</span>);<br>        coffee.brew();<br><br>        System.<span class="hljs-keyword">out</span>.println(<span class="hljs-string">"\nMaking Tea:"</span>);<br>        tea.brew();<br>    }<br>}</span></pre><p id="3041" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">By implementing the Template Method pattern, we achieved a solution where the overall algorithm for brewing a beverage is defined in the superclass, while specific steps can be customized by subclasses. This pattern promotes code reuse and consistency across subclasses while allowing for flexibility and customization where needed. Understanding and applying the Template Method pattern can greatly enhance the design and maintainability of software systems with common algorithmic structures.</p><h2 id="700a" class="nn no gr bb np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh oi oj ok bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Conclusion</h2><p id="138e" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms ol mu mv mw om my mz na on nc nd ne oo ng nh ni op nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Behavioral design patterns provide powerful solutions for managing interactions and responsibilities between objects in a software system. By focusing on how objects communicate and collaborate, these patterns enable developers to achieve flexibility, maintainability, and scalability in their designs.</p><p id="45cc" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Patterns like the Observer pattern facilitate efficient communication between objects by establishing one-to-many dependencies, ensuring that changes in one object are automatically reflected in others. The Strategy pattern allows for the dynamic selection of algorithms, enabling objects to vary their behavior independently from clients that use them. The Command pattern encapsulates requests as objects, enabling parameterization and decoupling of clients and receivers. The Chain of Responsibility pattern allows a request to be passed along a chain of handlers, offering a flexible and scalable approach to request handling. The Iterator pattern provides a uniform way to traverse collections without exposing their internal structure, promoting encapsulation and decoupling.</p><p id="d6bc" class="pw-post-body-paragraph mp mq gr mr b ms mt mu mv mw mx my mz na nb nc nd ne nf ng nh ni nj nk nl nm gk bg" data-selectable-paragraph="">Each behavioral pattern addresses specific challenges in software design, offering reusable and adaptable solutions to common problems. By understanding and applying these patterns effectively, developers can create robust, maintainable, and extensible software systems that meet the demands of complex and evolving requirements.</p></div>
